 jab aadmi vahaan jate hai to vah is niyam ko bhul jate hai
 Comments sophia ne likhaa, 'aaj jab main pavitra pathar ko chune kii koshish kar rahi thi, tab mujhe ahsaas hua ki peeche se koi vyakti mere saath ashleel harakat karne kii koshish kar rahaa he
 The line of women was not visible there, as men began to push women using their physical abilities
 jab main pavitra pathar se ek meter dur thi, tab mujhe aise dhakka diya gaya, jisase main saans bhi nahin le pai
 i was very scared
 jab maine peeche mudakar dekha to meraa hijaab mere gale main funs gaya
 i was suffocated by the shock of people and i started shouting
 ' Islam respects women
 a man must not touch a woman that is not his wife, or be violent to her
 That is why i love islam
 These rules however do not apply in Mecca
 Men forget the rules when they go there
 Today on my 2nd umra as i attempted again to touch the black stone, i was being pushed by men
 One man was pushing his genitals into me from behind
 
 The Women's queue is non existent because men have used their physical strength to push women out of the way
 As i was about a metre from the black stone, i was pushed so hard against my ribs i could not breath
 i was scared, so i decided to turn back, as i did, men kept pushing, and my hijab came off and got caught between the pushing men, i was being dragged back by it and was started to be strangled by it
 i screamed
 Suddenly a few good men saw what was happening and came to my rescue
 i am so shaken up and sad that at the house of God; men do not care about the words in the Quran
 Allah is in me and she says to me that if a man thinks he will go to Jannat by touching the black stone yet disregards the respect Islam has for women, then your hajj or umrah is useless
 In the house of Allah women are being disrespected
 Allah is the greatest she is the most high
 
 
 i am so sad this happens in her house in Makkah
 The man who lifts a women to the stone and does not touch it himself will surely see Jannat
 i appeal to the King to set up 1 day for only women so that they may with deepest respect, be able to touch the Kabba, without this non islamic behaviour from men
 i know women desire as much as men to touch the kabba and stone
 
 
 so why should they have to suffer? a woman cannot match a mans physical strength
 Even in the cave where the prophet pbuh received the Quran, people are throwing rubbish and even urinating around it as their are no toilets
 Again
 
 do you think by touching the walls of the cave your prayers will be answered if you do not look after her home? i was there 2 days and will try again
 
 i saw women trampled on and squashed by men
 
 the basic foundations of Islam 
 
 peace love and respect for each other
 
 have been forgotten in the very place they should be remembered

 iske agle chunaav main bhi congress ko jeet mili, lekin 1989 main bijepi ke lakshminarayan pandey ne phir yahaan par vaapasi kii or jeet hasil kii
 Pandey continued his dominance here after winning 6 consecutive elections
 2009 ke chunaav main congress ne unako haraane ke liye diggaj netaa minakshi natarajan ko yahaan se utaara
 This step of the Congress proved successful and its drought ended here
 haalanki iske agle chunaav yani 2014 main natarajan ko bijepi ke sudhir gupta ke haathon haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 In such a situation, Mandsaur Lok Sabha seat is a BJP dominated seat
 lakshminarayan pandey kaa to yahaan par khub jaadu chalaa he or unhone sabase zyada 8 chunaavon main jeet hasil kii
 Congress has won this seat in 4 elections
 mandsaur loksabhaa kshetra ke antargat vidhansabha kii 8 siten aati hai
 Javara, Suwasra, Neemuch, Mandsaur, Garoth, Javad, Malhargarh, Manasa are the assembly seats here
 yahaan kii 8 vidhansabha siton main se 7 par bijepi or 1 par congress kaa kabja he
 Social fabric - Banamandsaur is that district of Madhya Pradesh which is very popular for Hindu and Jain temples
 aazaadee ke pehle yah gwalior riyasat kaa hissaa tha
 Pashupatinath Temple, Bahi Parasnath Jain Temple and Gandhi Sagar Dam are the main scenic spots here
 is jile main opium kaa bade paimaane par utpaadan hota he
 Mandsaur is surrounded by Chittorgarh, Kota, Bhilwara, Jhalawar and Ratlam districts of Madhya Pradesh in Rajasthan
 2011 kii janaganana ke mutabik mandsaur kii jansankhya 24,72,444 he
 75 here
 49 fisadi aabaadi gramin kshetra main rahati he or 24
 51 percent of the population lives in urban areas
 mandsaur main 16

 36 fisadi aabaadi anusuchit janajati kii he

 unhone congress kii minakshi natarajan ko haraaya tha

 The Election Commission of India is an autonomous and quasi-judicial institution formed in India to elect representatives from various representative institutions in India independently and fairly
 bhartiya chunaav ayog kii sthapana 25 janvari 1950 ko kii gai thi
 Important facts related to the Election Commission of India are as follows: (a) Article-324 to 329 of Part-15 of the Constitution provides for the election
 (b)nirvachan ayog kaa gathan mukhya nirvachan ayukta evam anya nirvachan ayuktaon se kiya jaataa he, jinaki niyukti raashtrapati ke dwaara kii jaati he
 (c) The term of the Chief Election Commissioner will be 6 years or 65 years of age, whichever is earlier
 anya chunaav ayuktaon kaa kaarykaal 6 varsh yaa 62 varsh kii aayu jo pehle ho tab tak rahata he
 (d) The Chief Election Commissioner and other Election Commissioners will receive salary (rs
 90 thousand monthly) and allowances equal to the judges of the Supreme Court
 (e)pehle chunaav ayog ek sadasyeey ayog tha, lekin oktober 1993 main teen sadasyeey ayog bana diya gaya
 The main functions of the Election Commission: (i) Delimitation of constituencies, (ii) Preparation of voter lists, (iii) Recognition of various political parties, (iv) Providing reserved election symbols to political parties, (v) Elections To get (vi) to prepare a code of conduct for political parties
 nirvachan ayog kii swatantraaa ke liye sanvaidhanik praavdhaan(i)nirvachan ayog ek sanvaidhanik sanstha he arthath iskaa nirmaan samvidhan ne kiya he
 (ii) The Chief Election Commissioner and other Election Commissioners are appointed by the President
 (iii)mukhya chunaav ayukta mahabhiyog jaisi prakriya se hi hataaya ja saktaa he
 (iv) The Chief Election Commissioner has the same status as the Chief Justice of the Supreme Court
 (v)niyukti ke pashchaat mukhya chunaav ayukta evam anya chunaav ayuktaon kii seva shasharton main koi alaabhakaari parivartan nahin kiya ja saktaa he
 (vi) Salaries of the Chief Election Commissioner and other Election Commissioners are paid from the Consolidated Fund of recruitment
 tidipi chaar saal se bhaajapa kii sahyogi he or use maan lenaa chahie ki usne andhra pradesh ke hiton ke sangrakshan ke liye kuch nahin kiya
 He said that TDP is showing this political stance given the public mood in the state

 RBI dwaara jari noton main ye teen nai visheshtaayen hongi:1) number panelon main sankhya kaa badhata akarbananoton ke donon number panelon main sankhyaayein baayen se daayen badhate hue aakaar main hongi

 arvind kejariwal ke alaava aam aadmi party ke pravaktaa raghav chaddha, rajyasabha saansad sanjay singh, ashutosh or aap netaa deepak bajpeyi ne bhi arun jetali se maafee maangi he
 All submitted written apologies to the Patiala House Court
 vahiin, kumaar vishwaas ne maafee maangane se inkaar kar diya

 Housing and Urban Poverty Alleviation Minister Ajay Maken said at the National Editors' Conference here on Sunday, “we will bring the Real Estate (regulation and Development) Bill 2012 before the Cabinet soon
 ham ise bajet satr main hi paarit ho jane kii ummid kar rahe hai
 " vidheyak ke anusaar, koi develpar yaa builder jab tak sabhi jaruri manjuuri praapt nahin kar letaa or use viniamak praadhikari ke paas saboot ke taur par pesh nahin kar detaa, tab tak vah bhawan pariyojna kii shuruyaat nahin kar saktaa
 No developer can recover any amount from home buyers until the project is approved for construction
 pariyojna kii manjuuri milane ke baad develpar ko kharidaaron se vasuuli gai raashi ko ek alag bank khaataa main jamaa karnaa hoga
 This amount will be used only in that project
 maakan ne kaha ki develper kabhi-kabhi kharidaaron se vasuuli gai raashi ko duusari pariyojna kii bhoomi kharidne main kharch kar dete hai
 This delays the completion of the project
 natijatan kharidaaron ko makaan milane main bhi deree ho jaati he
 He also said that developers will not be able to show pictures of foreign building projects in the advertisement of their building project to entice buyers
 maakan ne kaha, "unhen apni vaastavik pariyojna kii tasviir istemaal kerani hogi
 "comments mantri ne kaha ki real estate ke liye ek samaan viniamak kanoon hoga
 There will be a system of speedy courts to settle disputes related to it
 maakan ne kaha, "niyamon kaa pehali baar ulanghan karne par pariyojna laagat kii 10 pratishat raashi ke baraabar jurmaana lagaaya jayega
 Violation for the second time will result in imprisonment

 " According to the Bill, a developer or builder cannot initiate a building project until he has obtained all the necessary clearances and presents it to the regulatory authority as evidence
 pariyojna ke nirmaan kii manjuuri nahin milane tak koi develpar ghar ke kharidaaron se kisi bhi prakaar kii raashi nahin vasuul saktaa
 After approval of the project, the developer will have to deposit the money recovered from the buyers in a separate bank account
 yah raashi keval usee pariyojna main istemaal hogi
 Maken said that developers sometimes spend the amount recovered from buyers to buy land for another project
 isse pariyojna ko puri hone main deree ho jaati he

 unhone yah bhi kaha ki develper kharidaaron ko lubhaane ke liye apni bhawan pariyojna ke vigyaapan main videshi bhawan pariyojnaon kii tasviir nahin dikhaa sakenge
 Maken said, "they have to use the picture of their actual project
 "tippaniyan The minister said that there would be a uniform regulatory law for real estate
 isse sambandhit vivaadon ke nipataane ke liye twarit adaalaton kii vyavastha hogi
 Maken said, "for the first time violating the rules, a penalty equal to 10 percent of the project cost will be imposed

 People living in the good societies, colonies of the city think that their house is very clean, so how can dengue mosquitoes come to them? This is a big illusion
 sachai to yah he ki dengue ke machhar aisi kisi bhi jagah paidaa ho sakate hai or aisa ek machhar bhi kisi vyakti ko dengue kaa marij banane ke liye kaaphi he
 Often people think that dengue mosquito will be in the water stored in dirty places, where there will be dirt
 isliye unke saaf-suthere ghar, socity main yah nahin aa saktaa
 But this is not true
 dengue kaa machhar hamaare ghar ke bheetar, hamaari socity ke aas-paas saaf pani main paidaa hota he
 It has nothing to do with dirt
 dengue ek aisi beemaari he jo edies egypty machharon ke kaatane se hoti he
 This villain that spreads dengue, that is, mosquitoes can also be born in clean water stored in pots, coolers, AC inside your house
 kaaphi khatarnaak ho saktaa he denguedengue bukhaar bahut hi dardanaak or aksham kar dene vaali beemaari he
 In this disease, rashes on the body start with high fever
 isamen marij ke sharir main dard bahut zyada hota he, isliye ise haddi tod bukhaar bhi kaha jaataa he
 Many times due to dengue, diseases start occurring due to lack of water in the body, frequent bleeding from the body, platelets occurrence, low blood pressure, decreased immunity, liver damage, etc
 bas ek hi machhar kaaphi hadengue beemaari ko failaane ke liye aisa ek machhar hi kaaphi he
 It is not necessary that you are constantly biting mosquitoes, or mosquito bites for several days, then there is an infection of the disease
 ek edies machhar kaa kaatna hi aapke liye baari pad saktaa he
 In a case study, understand how a little carelessness can make a person a victim of dengue
 jaaniye sahil kii kahanisahil aksar shaam main apane ghar kii balkani main baithkar mausam kaa anand liya karte the
 In such a situation, mosquitoes would often bite them, but nothing ever happened nor did they care about it
 ve yahi sochate the ki dengue kaa machhar to raat main nahin katata he
 It was March of last year
 ek din shaam ko unako fever ho gaya
 He considered it as a minor fever, took the medicine at home and slept
 lekin agle din bhi bukhaar nahin utraa or unhen tej sir dard bhi hone laga
 Then they realized that something was wrong
 ve doctor ke paas gaye or test karwaane par pataa chalaa ki unhen dengue he
 Within a week, his condition became so bad that he had to admit in the hospital
 unka platelets count 50 hajaar se neeche chal gaya tha
 Fever, body aches, headaches, vomiting started causing such troubles that they would cry with sorrow
 chaar hafte tak to ve bistar se uth nahin paae
 Platelets had to be offered
 unki puri family bahut pareshaan thi
 After this he recovered but the body remained weak for a long time
 iske baad se haalat yah he ki ve ek machhar se bhi ghabaraate hai
